};

Module!</font></strong></font></p>\r\n<p>\r\n\t<font face="Arial">&nbsp;</font></p>\r\n<p>\r\n\t<font face="Arial"><font size="2"><strong>Application of Workspaces</strong></font></font></p>\r\n<p>\r\n\t<font face="Arial" size="2">Workspaces are central to the design and functioning of KMSS, since most if not all corporate contents will be deposited into different workspaces eventually.&nbsp; They are set up for various collaboration workgroups to unify filing, discussion, external linking and access to various kinds of media and information in a single digital space.&nbsp; </font></p>\r\n<p>\r\n\t<font face="Arial" size="2">Colleagues are encouraged to collaborate and communicate within those workspaces they belong to.&nbsp; In doing so, work knowledge will not be hidden behind email archives and local drives which are not accessible by others for reference later.&nbsp; The use of workspaces will improve the Department\'s ability to leverage and preserve knowledge assets and cultivate a culture of collaboration and open communication.</font></p>\r\n<p>\r\n\t<font face="Arial" size="2">&nbsp;</font></p>\r\n<p>\r\n\t<font face="Arial"><font size="2"><strong>Features of Workspaces</strong></font></font></p>\r\n<p>\r\n\t<font face="Arial"><font size="2">A set of collaboration tools, such as shared folders, discussion forums, group calendar, workflow management and co-authoring functions, are available within workspaces.&nbsp; Appropriate access rights can be set up to protect the information stored in workspaces.<br />\r\n\t&nbsp;</font></font></p>\r\n<p>\r\n\t&nbsp;<font face="Arial"><font size="2"><strong>Contents in Workspaces</strong></font></font></p>\r\n<p>\r\n\t<font face="Arial"><font size="2">The KMSS can process, store and transmit classified data <strong>up to RESTRICTED level</strong>.&nbsp; No CONFIDENTIAL data or copyrighted materials should be deposited in {

if (weeklyNews != null)

if (dailyNews != null)
dailyNews.href += nonceValue;
}

}
if (h_Form=="E9077196440B29CF852567E500525B7F") {
var img=document.getElementById("h_pptSlideImg");
if (!img) {
var imgs=document.body.getElementsByTagName("img");
for (var i=0; i<imgs.length; i++) {
if (imgs[i].src.indexOf("/TMP")>0) {
img=imgs[i];
break;
}
}
}
if (img) {
var src=img.src;
var i1=src.indexOf("/$FILE");
var i2=src.indexOf("/TMP");
var i3=src.indexOf(".GIF");
if (i1 == -1 && i2 > 0 && i3 > 0) {
var n = parseInt(src.substring(i2+4));
img.style.display="none";
img.src = src.substring(0,i2) + "/$FILE/TMP" + (n+1) + ".GIF";
img.setAttribute("width","600");
img.style.display="block";
}
}
var sldBtn=qp_getElementsByClassName("SlideButton", "a");
for (var i=0; i < sldBtn.length; i++) {
var href=sldBtn[i].href;
if (href.charAt(href.length-1)=='.') {
var i2=href.indexOf(";TMP");
if (i2 > 0) {
var n = parseInt(href.substring(i2+4));
sldBtn[i].href = href.substring(0,i2) + ";TMP" + (n-3) + ".HTM";
}
}
}
}
logExit("onLoad_Handler");

function isBlogPlace(){
var ret = false;
if (!ret) ret = ( typeof window.G_PlaceType == "string" && window.G_PlaceType.toLowerCase() == "blog" );
if (!ret) ret = ( typeof window.c_BlogDate != "undefined" );
if (!ret) ret = isBlogPage();	
return ret;
}
function isBlogPage(){
var ret = false;
if (!ret) {
if (typeof window.c_Form == "string") {
ret = (window.c_Form.toLowerCase() == "qpreference" || window.c_Form.toLowerCase() == "blogentry")
}
}	
if (!ret) {
if ( typeof theForm != "undefined" && typeof theForm.c_Form != "undefined" && typeof theForm.c_Form.value == "string" ) {
ret = (theForm.c_Form.value.toLowerCase() == "qpreference" || theForm.c_Form.value.toLowerCase() == "blogentry");
}
}
return ret; 
}
function isWikiPage() {
var ret = false;
if (!ret) ret = ( typeof window.c_Form == "string" && window.c_Form.toLowerCase() == "wiki" );
if (!ret) ret = ( typeof theForm != "undefined" && typeof theForm.c_Form != "undefined" && typeof theForm.c_Form.value == "string" && theForm.c_Form.value.toLowerCase() == "wiki" );		
return ret;
}

var ret = false;

if (!ret) ret = ( typeof window.c_Form != "undefined" && typeof window.c_Form.value == "string" && window.c_Form.value.toLowerCase() == "wiki" );
if (!ret) ret = isWikiPage(); 
return ret;
}
function loadCKEditorConfig(){
var ckLoadLocation 	= window.G_JunctionLoc + "/qphtml/html/common/ckeditorload.js";	
script 		= 	document.createElement("script");
script.src	=	ckLoadLocation;
oHeadLoc 	= document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0];
if (oHeadLoc) oHeadLoc.appendChild(script);
}
if( (h_CurrentSkinName != "h_SetupSkin" && h_SetEditScene != 'h_TailorIntroRead' && h_CurrentSkinType == 'h_Edit') || isBlogPlace() ) {
if (typeof window.CKEDITOR == "undefined") {
var ckEditorLoc = "/qphtml/ckeditor/ckeditor.js";
var scriptSRC = window.G_JunctionLoc + ckEditorLoc;
var script = document.createElement("script");
script.src=scriptSRC;
script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = function(e){
if(e && e.type == "load" || /complete|loaded/.test(script.readyState)){
script.onload = script.onreadystatechange = null;
loadCKEditorConfig();
}
}
var oHeadLoc = document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0];
if (oHeadLoc) oHeadLoc.appendChild(script);
}
else{
loadCKEditorConfig();
}
}

if (oHtmlLoc[0]) {
oHtmlLoc[0].setAttribute("lang", window.G_Locale.substr(0,2));
}

}

function refreshForImage() {
if(typeof(Image) == 'undefined') {
window.location.reload();
}
};
var oldSelectedImage = new Image (10, 10);
var newSelectedImage = new Image (10, 10);
var currentRoomImage = new Image (10, 10);
var transparentImage = new Image (10, 10);
if(document.body.dir == "ltr")
currentRoomImage.src = "../../../../../qphtml/attachments/sitemaparrow.gif";
else if(document.body.dir == "rtl")
currentRoomImage.src = "../../../../../qphtml/attachments/sitemaparrow_rtl.gif";
transparentImage.src = "../../../../../qphtml/attachments/transparent.gif";
var intervalID;
var timeoutId;
document.write(generateRoomList());
startPolling();
function startPolling() { 
logEnter("startPolling");
intervalID = setInterval ('checkCurrentRoom()', 500);
clearTimeout(timeoutId);
logExit("startPolling"); 
};
function generateRoomList() { 
logEnter("generateRoomList");
szOutText = '<table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 border=0 width=100% summary=' + "This table contains the Quickr Sitemap." + '>';
szOutText+=		'<tr class="h-folderBanner-bg"><td colspan="2" class="h-roomHeader-text-bold" nowrap>';
szOutText+=			'<img src=' + transparentImage.src + ' width="1" height="2" alt="" border="0">';
szOutText+=			"Rooms in this place" + '<img src=' + transparentImage.src + ' width="1" height="3" alt="" border="0"></td></tr>';
szOutText+=		'<tr class="h-folderBanner-bg"><td colspan="2" class="h-roomHeader-text" nowrap>';
szOutText+=			'<img src=' + transparentImage.src + ' width="1" height="2" alt="" border="0">';
szOutText+=			"Click any room name to go there" + '<img src=' + transparentImage.src + ' width="1" height="3" alt="" border="0"></td></tr>';
szOutText+=		'<tr><td colspan="2"><img src=' + transparentImage.src + ' width="1" height="7" alt="" border="0"></td></tr>';
var szStr1 = "";
var nlen, szName = "", szSpaces;
var nWidth;
for (var i = 0; i < numRooms; i++)
{
nWidth = 5;
szName = h_RoomNames[i];
nlen = szName.length - 1;
while (nlen > 0)
{
if (szName.charAt(nlen) == '/')
nWidth += 10;
nlen--;
}
szName = szName.substring(szName.lastIndexOf('/') + 1);
if (h_RoomDbNames[i] == currentRoom.roomNsf) {
currentRoomIndex = i;
szStr1 +=	'<tr id="RoomRow' + i.toString(10) + '" ' + (h_ClientBrowser.isNetscape4()?'>':'class="h-roomSelected-bg">'); 
szStr1 +=		'<td class="h-room-text" nowrap valign="top">';
szStr1 +=			'<img src=' + transparentImage.src + ' width=' + nWidth + ' height="1" alt="" border="0">';
szStr1 +=			'<img name="CurrentRoom' + i.toString(10) + '" src=' + currentRoomImage.src + ' width=10 height=10 border=0 alt="' + "Selected Room";
szStr1 += 			((h_ClientBrowser.isGecko() || h_ClientBrowser.isSafari()) ? '" title="'+ "Selected Room" : '') + '">';
}
else {
szStr1 +=	'<tr id="RoomRow' + i.toString(10) + '" >';
szStr1 +=		'<td class="h-room-text" nowrap>';
szStr1 +=			'<img src=' + transparentImage.src + ' width=' + nWidth + ' height="1" alt="" border="0">';
szStr1 +=			'<img name="CurrentRoom' + i.toString(10) + '" src=' + transparentImage.src + ' width=10 height=10 border=0 alt="' + "Room";
szStr1 +=			((h_ClientBrowser.isGecko() || h_ClientBrowser.isSafari()) ? '" title="'+ "Room" : '') + '">';
}
if (typeof(window.opener.EnterRoom) == "undefined") {
szStr1 += '<a href=javascript:window.opener.dijit.byId("placelink").goToRoom("' + h_RoomDbNames[i] + '") onClick=javascript:changeCurrentRoom(' + 
i + ') class="h-room-text">' + szName + '</a>';
}
else {
szStr1 += '<a href=javascript:window.opener.EnterRoom("' + h_RoomDbNames[i] + '") onClick=javascript:changeCurrentRoom(' + 
i + ') class="h-room-text">' + szName + '</a>';
}
szStr1 += '</TD></TR>';
}
numRooms--;
szOutText += szStr1;
szOutText += "</table>";
return szOutText;
logExit("generateRoomList"); 
};
function changeCurrentRoom(newRoomIndex) { 
logEnter("changeCurrentRoom");
clearInterval(intervalID);
oldSelectedImage	= eval ("document.CurrentRoom" + currentRoomIndex.toString(10));
newSelectedImage	= eval ("document.CurrentRoom" + newRoomIndex.toString(10));
if (h_ClientBrowser.isIE()) {
var oldSelectedRow	= eval ("document.all.RoomRow" + currentRoomIndex.toString(10));
var newSelectedRow	= eval ("document.all.RoomRow" + newRoomIndex.toString(10));
}
else if (h_ClientBrowser.isGecko() || h_ClientBrowser.isSafari()) {
var oldSelectedRow	= eval ("pageGetElementById('RoomRow" + currentRoomIndex.toString(10) + "')");
var newSelectedRow	= eval ("pageGetElementById('RoomRow" + newRoomIndex.toString(10) + "')");
}
else if (h_ClientBrowser.isNetscape4()) {
var oldSelectedRow	= eval ("document.ids.RoomRow" + currentRoomIndex.toString(10));
var newSelectedRow	= eval ("document.ids.RoomRow" + newRoomIndex.toString(10));
}
oldSelectedImage.src	= transparentImage.src;
newSelectedImage.src	= currentRoomImage.src;
oldSelectedRow.className = "";
newSelectedRow.className = "h-roomSelected-bg";
oldSelectedImage.alt	= "Room";
newSelectedImage.alt = "Selected Room";
currentRoomIndex	= newRoomIndex;
timeoutId =	setTimeout("startPolling()", 5000);
logExit("changeCurrentRoom"); 
};
function checkCurrentRoom() { 
logEnter("checkCurrentRoom");
if (typeof(opener.currentRoom) != "object") {
return;
}
for (var i = 0; i <= numRooms; i++)	{
if (typeof(opener.currentRoom) == "object" && h_RoomDbNames[i] == opener.currentRoom.roomNsf) {
changeCurrentRoom(i);
break;
}
}
}
